m] ?? platform
    73 
    74     const hermesBaseUrl = Deno.env.get('HERMES_BASE_URL') || 'http://152.136.47.2:8642'
    75     const hermesApiKey = Deno.env.get('HERMES_API_KEY') || 'bWmhP67eBZsbta58h8QRKrZT0XcPh2NJ'
    76 
    77     // 请求 Hermes 生成平台授权二维码
    78     // 约定回复格式：
    79     //   <!--QR_URL:https://...--> 二维码图片地址
    80     //   <!--SESSION_ID:xxxxxxxx--> 会话 ID，用于后续轮询授权状态
    81     const prompt = `请为用户生成${platformLabel}账号「${account_name}」的授权绑定二维码。
    82 用户将使用该二维码在${platformLabel}客户端完成扫码授权，授权后系统将自动同步该账号数据。
    83 
    84 请在回复末尾追加以下格式的标记（不要省略）：
    85 <!--QR_URL:二维码图片的完整URL-->
    86 <!--SESSION_ID:授权会话ID-->
    87 
    88 如果暂时无法生成，请说明原因。`
    89 
    90     const upstream = await fetch(`${hermesBaseUrl}/v1/chat/completions`, {
    91       method: 'POST',
    92       headers: {
    93         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    94         'Authorization': `Bearer ${hermesApiKey}`,
    95       },
    96       body: JSON.stringify({
    97         model: 'hermes-agent',
    98         messages: [
    99           {
   100             role: 'system',
   101             content: '你是 Luna AI 平台的 Hermes Agent，负责处理自媒体账号授权绑定。当用户请求生成授权二维码时，调用相应平台的 MCP 工具创建授权会话，并按约定格式返回二维码 URL 和 Session ID。'
   102           },
   103           {role: 'user', content: prompt}
   104         ],
   105         stream: false,
   106         max_tokens: 1024,
   107       }),
   108     })
   109 
   110     if (!upstream.ok) {
   111       const errText = await upstream.text().catch(() => '')
   112       console.error('Hermes API 错误:', upstream.status, errText)
   113       return Response.json(
   114         {error: `Hermes 服务异常 (${upstream.status})`, hermesError: errText},
   115         {status: 502, headers: corsHeaders}
   116       )
   117     }
   118 
   119     const data = await upstream.json()
   120     const reply: string = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? ''
   121     console.log('Hermes 回复:', reply.slice(0, 500))
   122 
   123     const qrUrl = extractQrUrl(reply)
   124     const sessionId = extractSessionId(reply)
   125 
   126     // 清洗掉约定标记，得到展示给用户的说明文字
   127     const displayText = reply
   128       .replace(QR_URL_RE, '')
   129       .replace(SESSION_ID_RE, '')
   130       .trim()
   131 
   132     if (!qrUrl) {
   133       // Hermes 未返回二维码，将原始回复透传给前端展示
   134       return Response.json(
   135         {
   136           success: false,
   137           qrUrl: null,
   138           sessionId: null,
   139           message: displayText || 'Hermes 暂时无法生成二维码，请稍后重试。',
   140           rawReply: reply,
   141         },
   142         {headers: corsHeaders}
   143       )
   144     }
   145 
   146     return Response.json(
   147       {
   148         success: true,
   149         qrUrl,
   150         sessionId,
   151         message: displayText,
   152       },
   153       {headers: corsHeaders}
   154     )
   155   } catch (err) {
   156     console.error('hermes-get-binding-qrcode 错误:', err)
   157     return Response.json(
   158       {error: String(err)},
   159       {status: 500, headers: corsHeaders}
   160     )
   161   }
   162 })

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: 项目中与 Hermes 通信的链路如下：

---

## 1. 通信协议

| 项 | 内容 |
|---|---|
| **地址** | `http://152.136.47.2:8642`（默认，可通过环境变量覆盖） |
| **接口** | `POST /v1/chat/completions` |
| **格式** | OpenAI 兼容格式 |
| **鉴权** | `Authorization: Bearer {HERMES_API_KEY}` |
| **模型** | `hermes-agent` |

---

## 2. 请求格式（Deno fetch）

```typescript
const hermesRes = await fetch(`${HERMES_BASE_URL}/v1/chat/completions`, {
  method: 'POST',
  headers: {
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${HERMES_API_KEY}`,
    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    model: 'hermes-agent',
    messages: [
      { role: 'system', content: '系统人设...' },
      { role: 'user', content: '用户消息...' }
    ],
    stream: false,
    max_tokens: 1024
  })
})
```

---

## 3. 响应格式

```json
{
  "choices": [{
    "message": {
      "role": "assistant",
      "content": "Hermes 的回复文本..."
    }
  }]
}
```

取回复：`hermesData?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content`

---

## 4. 项目中有 3 个地方调用 Hermes

| Edge Function | 用途 |
|---|---|
| `customer_service` | 客服智能对话（支持文字+图片） |
| `hermes-get-binding-qrcode` | 生成小红书等平台的授权绑定二维码（Hermes 调用 MCP 工具） |
| `update_analytics` | 异步生成运营简报 |

---

## 5. Hermes 的特殊能力（MCP 工具）

Hermes 与 MiniMax 不同——**Hermes 持有 MCP（Model Context Protocol）工具权限**，比如：
- 调用平台 OAuth 流程生成授权二维码
- 访问外部数据源生成运营简报

而 `luna_guardian` 调用的 MiniMax 只是纯文本对话模型，没有工具调用能力。

---

**简单说**：  
→ Hermes 在 `152.136.47.2:8642` 这台服务器上  
→ 走标准 OpenAI 接口格式  
→ 带 API Key + 系统人设 + 用户消息  
→ 返回文本回复

如果你想把 Hermes 集成到 Luna 的聊天流程里（比如让 Luna 在某些场景下转交 Hermes 处理），或者想了解 Hermes 的 MCP 工具具体有哪些，我可以进一步展开。

   171 // ── 主页面 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172 function WorkbenchPage() {
   173   const {user, profile} = useAuth()
   174   const [messages, setMessages] = useState<ChatMessage[]>([WELCOME])
   175   const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('')
   176   // pendingAttachment: image has tempPath for preview; file has name only
   177   const [pendingAttachment, setPendingAttachment] = useState<{
   178     type: 'image' | 'file'
   179     tempPath: string    // image preview path (empty for file)
   180     publicUrl: string   // uploaded URL
   181     name: string        // file name (used for file type display)
   182   } | null>(null)
   183   const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false)
   184   const [sending, setSending] = useState(false)
   185 
   186   useShareAppMessage(() => ({title: 'Luna AI — 内容创作工作台'}))
   187   useShareTimeline(() => ({title: 'Luna AI — 内容创作工作台'}))
   188 
   189   const lastMsgId = useMemo(() => {
   190     const last = messages[messages.length - 1]
   191     return last ? `msg_${last.id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_')}` : ''
   192   }, [messages])
   193 
   194   // ── 发送消息 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   195   const handleSend = useCallback(async (quickText?: string) => {
   196     const text = (quickText ?? inputText).trim()
   197     const attachUrl = pendingAttachment?.publicUrl || ''
   198     const attachName = pendingAttachment?.name || ''
   199     const isImageAttach = pendingAttachment?.type === 'image'
   200     if (!text && !attachUrl) return
   201     if (sending || !user) return
   202 
   203     // 只有附件没有文字时，自动补充描述让 Luna 知道有素材要处理
   204     const effectiveText = text || (isImageAttach
   205       ? `请根据这张图片帮我生成多平台内容`
   206       : `请根据上传的文件「${attachName}」帮我生成多平台内容`)
   207 
   208     setInputText('')
   209     setPendingAttachment(null)
   210     setSending(true)
   211 
   212     const userMsg: ChatMessage = {
   213       id: `u_${Date.now()}`,
   214       role: 'user',
   215       content: text || (isImageAttach ? '[图片]' : `[文件] ${attachName}`),
   216       image_url: isImageAttach ? attachUrl : null,
   217       attachName: !isImageAttach && attachUrl ? attachName : undefined,
   218       created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   219     }
   220     // 用正式消息替换上传预览气泡
   221     setMessages((prev) => [...prev.filter((m) => m.id !== 'upload_preview'), userMsg])
   222 
   223     try {
   224       const session = await supabase.auth.getSession()
   225       const token = session.data.session?.access_token
   226 
   227       const history = messages
   228         .filter((m) => !m.isPending && (m.role === 'user' || (m.role === 'assistant' && !m.taskCard && !m.resultCard)))
   229         .filter((m) => m.content && m.content.trim())
   230         .slice(-10)
   231         .map((m) => ({role: m.role, content: m.content}))
   232 
   233       const body: Record<string, unknown> = {
   234         user_id: user.id,
   235         user_message: effectiveText,
   236         history,
   237         platforms: ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号'],
   238         ...(attachUrl && isImageAttach ? {material_images: [attachUrl], material_text: effectiveText} : {}),
   239         ...(attachUrl && !isImageAttach ? {material_file_url: attachUrl, material_text: effectiveText} : {}),
   240       }
   241 
   242       const {data, error} = await supabase.functions.invoke('luna_guardian', {
   243         body,
   244         headers: token ? {Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`} : {},
   245       })
   246 
   247       if (error) {
   248         const errMsg = await error?.context?.text?.()
   249         throw new Error(errMsg || error.message)
   250       }
   251 
   252       const taskType: TaskType = data?.task_type || 'normal_chat'
   253       const reply: string = data?.reply || ''
   254       const result = data?.result || null
   255       const materialId: string | null = data?.material_id || null
   256 
   257       if ((taskType === 'material_package' || taskType === 'direction_package'
   258         || taskType === 'copy_rewrite' || taskType === 'video_script' || taskType === 'advice_only')
   259         && !result) {
   260         const platforms = ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
   261         const taskCard: TaskCard = {
   262           platform: platforms,
   263           goal: '品牌曝光与内容传播',
   264           source: attachUrl
   265             ? (isImageAttach ? '用户上传图片 + 文字描述' : `上传文件「${pendingAttachment?.name || '素材文件'}」`)
   266             : (text ? `"${text.slice(0, 30)}"` : '用户描述'),
   267           output: taskType === 'video_script' ? '短视频脚本' : taskType === 'copy_rewrite' ? '多平台改写文案' : '多平台素材包（标题 / 正文 / 话题标签 / 投放建议）',
   268           taskType,
   269           rawBody: body,
   270         }
   271         setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
   272           id: `t_${Date.now()}`,
   273           role: 'assistant',
   274           content: reply || '我已理解你的任务，请确认以下方案后开始生成：',
   275           taskCard,
   276           created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   277         }])
   278       } else if (result && materialId) {
   279         const platforms = Object.keys(result)
   280         const firstPlatform = platforms[0] || '小红书'
   281         const firstResult = result[firstPlatform] || {}
   282         const summaryTitle = Array.isArray(firstResult.titles) ? (firstResult.titles as string[])[0] : '素材包已生成'
   283         setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
   284           id: `r_${Date.now()}`,
   285           role: 'assistant',
   286           content: reply,
   287           resultCard: {materialId, title: summaryTitle, platforms, summary: reply},
   288           created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   289         }])
   290       } else {
   291         setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
   292           id: `a_${Date.now()}`,
   293           role: 'assistant',
   294           content: reply || '抱歉，暂时无法回复，请稍后再试。',
   295           created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   296         }])
   297       }
   298     } catch {
   299       Taro.showToast({title: '发送失败，请重试', icon: 'none'})
   300       setMessages((prev) => prev.filter((m) => m.id !== userMsg.id))
   301     } finally {
   302       setSending(false)
   303     }
   304   }, [inputText, pendingAttachment, sending, user, messages])
   305 
   306   // ── 任务卡：直接生成 ────────────────────────────────────────────
   307   const handleDirectGenerate = useCallback(async (taskCard: TaskCard) => {
   308     if (sending || !user) return
   309     setSending(true)
   310     Taro.showToast({title: '生成中，请稍候…', icon: 'none', duration: 3000})
   311     try {
   312       const session = await supabase.auth.getSession()
   313       const token = session.data.session?.access_token
   314       const body: Record<string, unknown> = {
   315         ...taskCard.rawBody,
   316         user_id: user.id,
   317         mode: taskCard.taskType === 'direction_package' ? 'direction' : 'material',
   318         platforms: taskCard.platform,
   319       }
   320       const {data, error} = await supabase.functions.invoke('luna_guardian', {
   321         body,
   322         headers: token ? {Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`} : {},
   323       })
   324       if (error) {
   325         const errMsg = await error?.context?.text?.()
   326         throw new Error(errMsg || error.message)
   327       }
   328       const result = data?.result || null
   329       const materialId: string | null = data?.material_id || null
   330       const reply: string = data?.reply || '已生成完成'
   331       if (result && materialId) {
   332         const platforms = Object.keys(result)
   333         const firstPlatform = platforms[0] || '小红书'
   334         const firstResult = result[firstPlatform] || {}
   335         const summaryTitle = Array.isArray(firstResult.titles) ? (firstResult.titles as string[])[0] : '素材包已生成'
   336         setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
   337           id: `r_${Date.now()}`,
   338           role: 'assistant',
   339           content: reply,
   340           resultCard: {materialId, title: summaryTitle, platforms, summary: reply},
   341           created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   342         }])
   343       } else {
   344         setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
   345           id: `a_${Date.now()}`,
   346           role: 'assistant',
   347           content: data?.reply || '生成完成，但未能获取结果，请重试。',
   348           created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   349         }])
   350       }
   351     } catch {
   352       Taro.showToast({title: '生成失败，请重试', icon: 'none'})
   353     } finally {
   354       setSending(false)
   355     }
   356   }, [sending, user])
   357

   362   }

   370       created_at: new Date().toISOString(),

    35 登录账号、扫码登录、Cookie搬运、代理/绕风控、采集后台数据、获取私有播放量/访客/曝光/转化数据、自动发布、自动推送、自动评论、自动私信、批量养号、刷量、声称已读取平台后台数据。
    36 
    37 回复风格：专业亲切，简洁有力，中文为主。`
    38 
    39 // ── 安保层专用 Prompt（灰色地带语义判断，让 LLM 返回 JSON）────────
    40 const GUARD_JUDGE_PROMPT = `你是 Luna 的安保判断模块。请根据以下判断公式，对用户输入进行意图分类，返回严格 JSON。
    41 
    42 【判断公式】
    43 - 平台词 + 创作词 → action: "allow_chat" 或 "allow_generate"
    44 - 平台词 + 账号/采集/自动化词 → action: "safe_redirect"
    45 - 平台词 + 数据分析词 + 用户提供了数据 → action: "allow_generate"
    46 - 平台词 + 数据分析词 + 要 Luna 去抓后台 → action: "safe_redirect"
    47 - 意图不明确 → action: "ask_clarify"
    48 
    49 【平台白名单】小红书、抖音、视频号、公众号、快手、微博、B站、知乎
    50 【创作动作白名单】写、生成、改写、润色、优化、起标题、想选题、做脚本、做口播、做封面建议、做标签、做投放建议、做内容规划、做素材包、做内容矩阵、做账号定位
    51 【内容对象白名单】文案、标题、脚本、选题、口播稿、封面、图片提示词、素材包、内容方案、推广方案、投放建议、标签、话题、栏目、账号定位、人设、卖点、产品介绍
    52 【数据来源白名单】用户手动输入、用户上传图片/视频/文案/表格/截图、用户提供公开链接、公开网页、公开榜单、搜索引擎公开结果
    53 
    54 【严格禁止】登录账号、扫码、Cookie、代理、绕风控、采集后台、私有播放量/访客/曝光/转化、自动发布、自动推送、自动评论、自动私信、批量养号、刷量
    55 
    56 【重要】白名单优先：对于正常创作请求，即使包含平台词，也应 allow，不要过度拦截。
    57 
    58 只输出 JSON，格式：
    59 {"action":"allow_chat|allow_generate|ask_clarify|safe_redirect","task_type":"normal_chat|creative_chat|material_package|direction_package|copy_rewrite|video_script|advice_only|need_more_info","reason":"一句话说明判断依据"}`
    60 
    61 // ── 白名单快通道 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    62 // 平台词
    63 const WL_PLATFORMS = /小红书|抖音|视频号|公众号|快手|微博|B站|知乎/
    64 // 创作动作词
    65 const WL_ACTIONS = /写|生成|改写|润色|优化|起标题|想选题|做脚本|做口播|做封面|做标签|做投放|做内容|做素材|做矩阵|做账号定位|帮我写|帮我做|帮我生成|帮我想|整理|看看|看一下|分析/
    66 // 内容对象词
    67 const WL_OBJECTS = /文案|标题|脚本|选题|口播稿|封面|图片提示词|素材包|内容方案|推广方案|投放建议|话题标签|账号定位|人设|卖点|产品介绍|内容矩阵|种草|笔记|内容规划|内容|发布时间|最佳时间|内容方向|公开链接/
    68 // 通用创作意图词（不需要平台词也放行）
    69 const WL_GENERIC_CREATE = /(帮我|请|我想|给我).{0,10}(写|生成|做|创作|策划|规划|起|想|整理|看看|分析).{0,15}(文案|脚本|标题|内容|素材|笔记|方案|口播|封面|方向|建议)/
    70 
    71 /**
    72  * 白名单检查：命中返回处理动作，未命中返回 null
    73  */
    74 function checkWhitelist(text: string): 'allow_chat' | 'allow_generate' | null {
    75   // 纯咨询/讨论类（含平台词且为疑问/讨论语气，未命中黑名单）→ 直接对话放行
    76   if (WL_PLATFORMS.test(text) && /[吗？]|怎么样|好不好|值不值|还能不能|能不能|有没有|呢/.test(text) && !checkBlacklist(text)) {
    77     return 'allow_chat'
    78   }
    79   // 明确的创作建议/时间/方案类请求（即使没有平台词）→ 直接放行
    80   const timeKeywords = ['发布时间', '最佳时间', '发内容时间', '发布时间建议', '最佳发布时间', '发布时间规划']
    81   if (timeKeywords.some((kw) => text.includes(kw))) return 'allow_chat'
    82   // 通用创作意图（不含平台词也放行）
    83   if (WL_GENERIC_CREATE.test(text)) return 'allow_generate'
    84   // 平台词 + (创作动作词 或 内容对象词) → 放行
    85   if (WL_PLATFORMS.test(text) && (WL_ACTIONS.test(text) || WL_OBJECTS.test(text))) {
    86     // 含素材包/方向/脚本/内容关键词 → allow_generate（需要生成结构化内容）
    87     if (/素材包|内容方案|脚本|口播稿|内容矩阵|内容方向|发布时间|最佳时间/.test(text)) return 'allow_generate'
    88     return 'allow_chat'
    89   }
    90   // 纯创作对象词（不含平台词）→ 放行为对话
    91   if (WL_OBJECTS.test(text) && WL_ACTIONS.test(text)) return 'allow_chat'
    92   return null
    93 }
    94

    99   /扫码.{0,6}(登录|绑定|授权)/,

   123 function checkBlacklist(text: string): boolean {
   124   const lower = text.toLowerCase()
   125   return BLACKLIST_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(lower))
   126 }
   127 
   128 // ── 处理动作类型 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129 type GuardAction = 'allow_chat' | 'allow_generate' | 'ask_clarify' | 'safe_redirect' | 'sanitize_output'
   130 
   131 // ── 任务类型 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   132 type TaskType =
   133   | 'normal_chat'
   134   | 'creative_chat'
   135   | 'material_package'
   136   | 'direction_package'
   137   | 'copy_rewrite'
   138   | 'video_script'
   139   | 'advice_only'
   140   | 'need_more_info'
   141 
   142 // ── 任务类型推断（用于白名单快通道命中后） ───────────────────────
   143 function inferTaskTypeFromText(text: string): TaskType {
   144   if (/素材包|多平台素材|生成素材/.test(text)) return 'material_package'
   145   if (/从方向|行业方向|热点方向|趋势分析|帮我分析.{0,6}(行业|赛道|方向)/.test(text)) return 'direction_package'
   146   if (/改写|优化文案|改得更|改成|改一下这.{0,4}文案|润色/.test(text)) return 'copy_rewrite'
   147   if (/(短视频|视频).{0,6}脚本|脚本.{0,6}(抖音|视频号|短视频)|帮我.{0,6}脚本/.test(text)) return 'video_script'
   148   if (/投放建议|广告建议|投放策略|怎么投放/.test(text)) return 'advice_only'
   149   if (/(小红书|抖音|视频号|公众号|快手|微博|B站|知乎).{0,20}(文案|内容|笔记|种草|脚本|方向|选题|标题|封面|配图|口播)/.test(text)) return 'creative_chat'
   150   if (/(帮我|生成|写|做|创作).{0,15}(文案|内容|笔记|脚本|标题|方向|选题|口播)/.test(text)) return 'creative_chat'
   151   if (/账号定位|人设规划|内容矩阵|选题规划/.test(text)) return 'advice_only'
   152   return 'normal_chat'
   153 }
   154 
   155 function inferTaskType(body: Record<string, unknown>): TaskType {
   156   const mode = body.mode as string | undefined
   157   if (mode === 'material') {
   158     const text = (body.material_text as string || '').trim()
   159     const images = (body.material_images as string[] || [])
   160     const fileUrl = (body.material_file_url as string || '').trim()
   161     if (!text && !images.length && !fileUrl) return 'need_more_info'
   162     return 'material_package'
   163   }
   164   if (mode === 'direction') {
   165     const industry = (body.industry as string || '').trim()
   166     if (!industry) return 'need_more_info'
   167     return 'direction_package'
   168   }
   169   // 有图片或文件附件时，直接识别为素材包任务（无需依赖 user_message 内容）
   170   const hasImages = Array.isArray(body.material_images) && (body.material_images as string[]).length > 0
   171   const hasFile = !!(body.material_file_url as string || '').trim()
   172   if (hasImages || hasFile) return 'material_package'
   173 
   174   const userMessage = (body.user_message as string || body.material_text as string || '').trim()
   175   if (!userMessage) return 'normal_chat'
   176   return inferTaskTypeFromText(userMessage)
   177 }

   199 function buildPackagePrompt(taskType: TaskType, body: Record<string, unknown>): string {
   200   const platforms: string[] = (body.platforms as string[]) || ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
   201   const goal = (body.goal as string) || '品牌曝光'
   202   const materialText = (body.material_text as string) || (body.user_message as string) || ''
   203   const images = (body.material_images as string[]) || []
   204   const industry = (body.industry as string) || ''
   205   const platformList = platforms.join('、')
   206 
   207   if (taskType === 'material_package') {
   208     const imageNote = images.length > 0 ? `\n用户还上传了 ${images.length} 张图片/视频作为素材参考。` : ''
   209     const fileUrl = (body.material_file_url as string || '').trim()
   210     const fileNote = fileUrl ? `\n用户上传了文件素材，文件地址：${fileUrl}，请基于该文件内容生成多平台内容方案。` : ''
   211     return `你是 Luna，专业的多平台内容策略师。\n\n用户提供的素材：\n${materialText || '（用户上传了附件素材）'}${imageNote}${fileNote}\n\n目标平台：${platformList}\n投放目标：${goal}\n\n请为每个目标平台分别生成完整的内容方案。\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`
   212   }
   213   if (taskType === 'direction_package') {
   214     return `你是 Luna，专业的多平台内容策略师，擅长热点趋势分析。\n\n用户的行业方向：${industry}\n目标平台：${platformList}\n投放目标：${goal}\n\n请基于该行业公开信息、平台内容规律和当前热点趋势生成多平台内容素材包。\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`
   215   }
   216   if (taskType === 'copy_rewrite') {
   217     return `你是 Luna，专业文案优化师。请对以下内容进行多平台文案改写：\n\n${materialText}\n\n目标平台：${platformList}\n\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`
   218   }
   219   if (taskType === 'video_script') {
   220     return `你是 Luna，专业短视频脚本创作师。请为以下内容生成短视频脚本：\n\n${materialText || industry}\n\n目标平台：${platformList}\n\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`
   221   }
   222   if (taskType === 'advice_only') {
   223     return `你是 Luna，专业投放策略顾问。请针对以下内容给出详细投放建议：\n\n${materialText || industry}\n\n目标平台：${platformList}\n投放目标：${goal}\n\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`
   224   }
   225   return materialText || industry
   226 }

   228 // ── JSON 提取与轻量修复 ───────────────────────────────────────────
   229 const ALL_PLATFORMS = ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
   230 
   231 function extractJSON(text: string): Record<string, unknown> | null {
   232   try { return JSON.parse(text) } catch { /* noop */ }
   233   const codeBlock = text.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]+?)```/)
   234   if (codeBlock) { try { return JSON.parse(codeBlock[1]) } catch { /* noop */ } }
   235   const braceMatch = text.match(/\{[\s\S]+\}/)
   236   if (braceMatch) { try { return JSON.parse(braceMatch[0]) } catch { /* noop */ } }
   237   return null
   238 }

   240 function repairPlatformResult(raw: Record<string, unknown>, requestedPlatforms: string[]): Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> {
   241   const result: Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> = {}
   242   const targetPlatforms = requestedPlatforms.length > 0 ? requestedPlatforms : ALL_PLATFORMS
   243   for (const platform of targetPlatforms) {
   244     const src = (raw[platform] || {}) as Record<string, unknown>
   245     result[platform] = {
   246       titles: Array.isArray(src.titles) ? src.titles : ['标题待生成'],
   247       body: typeof src.body === 'string' ? src.body : '内容待生成，请重试。',
   248       cover_suggestion: typeof src.cover_suggestion === 'string' ? src.cover_suggestion : '建议使用高质量产品图或人物出镜图',
   249       image_prompts: Array.isArray(src.image_prompts) ? src.image_prompts : [],
   250       hashtags: Array.isArray(src.hashtags) ? src.hashtags : [],
   251       best_time: typeof src.best_time === 'string' ? src.best_time : '工作日晚间 19:00-22:00',
   252       ad_advice: typeof src.ad_advice === 'string' ? src.ad_advice : '建议从小预算测试，找到最优人群定向后逐步放量。',
   253       risk_warning: typeof src.risk_warning === 'string' ? src.risk_warning : 'Luna 基于公开信息生成建议，请在发布前自行核实内容合规性。',
   254     }
   255   }
   256   return result
   257 }

   259 // ── 调用 MiniMax API ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   260 // 异常内容检测（只检测明确的客服/系统类非预期回复）
   261 const ABNORMAL_KEYWORDS = ['换绑手机号', '联系客服', '工单号', '联系我们处理', '访问被拒绝', '权限不足', '无效的API']
   262 
   263 function looksAbnormal(text: string): boolean {
   264   if (!text || text.trim().length < 5) return true
   265   return ABNORMAL_KEYWORDS.some((k) => text.includes(k))
   266 }
   267 
   268 // MiniMax M2.7 会在 content 中输出 <thinking>/<think> 思维链，需剥离
   269 function stripThinking(text: string): string {
   270   return text
   271     .replace(/<thinking>[\s\S]*?<\/thinking>/g, '')
   272     .replace(/<think>[\s\S]*?<\/think>/g, '')
   273     .trim()
   274 }
   275 
   276 async function callMiniMax(
   277   message: string,
   278   history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>,
   279   systemPrompt: string,
   280 ): Promise<string> {
   281   const apiKey = Deno.env.get('MINIMAX_API_KEY')
   282   const baseUrl = (Deno.env.get('MINIMAX_BASE_URL') || 'https://api.minimaxi.com/v1').replace(/\/$/, '')
   283 
   284   const messages = [
   285     {role: 'system', content: systemPrompt},
   286     ...history.slice(-10),
   287     {role: 'user', content: message},
   288   ]
   289 
   290   const res = await fetch(`${baseUrl}/chat/completions`, {
   291     method: 'POST',
   292     headers: {
   293       'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   294       'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   295     },
   296     body: JSON.stringify({
   297       model: 'MiniMax-M2.7-highspeed',
   298       messages,
   299       temperature: 0.7,
   300       max_tokens: 4096,
   301     }),
   302   })
   303 
   304   if (!res.ok) {
   305     const errText = await res.text()
   306     throw new Error(`MiniMax HTTP ${res.status}: ${errText}`)
   307   }
   308 
   309   const data = await res.json()
   310   const rawContent = data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || ''
   311   const content = stripThinking(rawContent)
   312   console.log('[MiniMax raw]', rawContent.slice(0, 300))
   313   console.log('[MiniMax stripped]', content.slice(0, 300))
   314 
   315   if (looksAbnormal(content)) {
   316     throw new Error(`MiniMax returned abnormal content: ${content.slice(0, 100)}`)
   317   }
   318 
   319   return content
   320 }
   321 
   322 // ── 灰色地带：让 LLM 做语义判断（返回结构化 JSON）────────────────
   323 async function llmJudge(
   324   userInput: string,
   325   history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>,
   326 ): Promise<{action: GuardAction; task_type: TaskType; reason: string}> {
   327   let raw = ''
   328   try {
   329     raw = await callMiniMax(
   330       `请判断以下用户输入的意图：\n\n"${userInput}"\n\n只返回 JSON，不要其他内容。`,
   331       history,
   332       GUARD_JUDGE_PROMPT,
   333     )
   334   } catch (e) {
   335     console.error('[llmJudge] callMiniMax failed:', e)

的设计\n\n这个函数被 luna_guardian 内部调用（supabase.functions.invoke），负责：\n1. 构建发给 Hermes 的 messages\n2. 把 attachments 整理进 messages 或 prompt\n3. 调用 Hermes\n4. 返回 { reply, model, upstream: \'hermes\', raw 函数。\n\n实际上，把 Hermes 调用逻辑直接写在 luna_guardian 里更简单，不需要额外的 Edge Function。但用户要求"新增或修正一个 luna_hermes_chat Edge Function，专门调用 Hermes"。\n\n所以：\n- `luna_hermes_chat` 作为独立的 Edge Function 存在\n- `luna_guardian` \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\')}`,\n    \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\'\n  },\n  body: JSON.stringify({...})\n})\n```\n\n这样 HERMES_API_KEY 只在 luna_hermes_chat 里用，luna_guardian 看不到它，也不会暴露给前端。\n\n### attachments metadata 设计\n\n前端发给 luna_guardian 的 payload：\n```json\n{\n  "user_id": "xxx",\n  "user_message": "根据这张图生成小红书内容",\n  "attachments": luna_hermes_chat。\n\n### 前端改动\n\n当前前端：\n- `pendingAttachment` 只存一个附件\n- 上传到 cs-images bucket\n- 发送时传 `material_images: [url]` 或 `material_file_url: url`\n\n需要改成：\n- `pendingAttachment` 改为存储 `attachments`，同时兼容旧的 `material_images` / `material_file_url`\n3. 内部统一为 `AttachmentMeta[]` 格式\n\n### 文件上传时 mime_type 和 size 的获取\n\n在 `handlePickAttachment` 里，上传成功后需要补充 mime_type 和 size：\n- `file.type` 或从文件名推断\n- `file.size`（MiniProgramFileInput 可能有 size 字段）\n\n从 upload.ts 看，MiniProgramFileInput 有 `tempFilePath`, `name`, `type`, `size` 等字段。\n\n让我整理一下前端 `pendingAttachment` 的新类型：\n```typescript\ninterface AttachmentMeta {\n  type: \'image\' | \'file\' | \'video\'\n  file_url: string\n  file_key: string\n  mime_type: string\n  file_type: string  // 扩展名\n  name: string\n \'user\',\n  content: imageUrl\n    ? `${message}（用户同时发送了一张图片：${imageUrl}，请根据图片内容给出建议）`\n    : message\n}\n```\n\n所以 customer_service 是用 URL 字符串嵌入 content，而不是 `{type: \'image_url\'}` 格式。\n\n考虑到不确定 Hermes 是否支持 OpenAI 的多模态格式，我先用文本+URL的方式，更稳定。\n\n### luna_hermes_chat 接受的参数\n\n```typescript\n{\n  system_prompt: string,      // Luna 系统 prompt\n  messages: Array<{role, content}>,  // 对话历史\n string,\n}\n```\n\n返回：\n```typescript\n{\n  reply: string,\n  model: \'hermes-agent\',\n  upstream: \'hermes\',\n  raw: string,\n}\n```\n\n注意：luna_hermes_chat 只负责调 Hermes 返回文本，JSON 解析和 materials 保存由 luna_guardian 做。\n\n### 实际流程：\n\n`luna_guardian` 收到请求 → 安保判断 → 构建 prompt 或 messages → 调用 `luna_hermes_chat` → 获取 reply → JSON 解析（素材包任务）→ 保存 materials → 返回前端\n\n这样 luna_hermes_chat 就是一个纯粹的 "Hermes 调用适配器"，不涉及业务逻辑。\n\n现在开始编写代码。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

Thought: **Step 1：新建 `luna_hermes_chat`**

Created File with Text:
```
/**
 * luna_hermes_chat — Hermes 调用适配器
 *
 * 职责：
 *  1. 接收 luna_guardian 路由过来的请求（system_prompt / messages / task_type / attachments / 生成参数）
 *  2. 将 attachments 按类型整理进 Hermes prompt
 *     - 图片：在 user 消息末尾追加 "用户附上了图片：<url>"（Hermes 不支持 image_url 对象）
 *     - 文档：追加 "用户附上了文件「name」，地址：<url>，请基于该文件内容生成"
 *     - 视频：第一版提示用户补充说明，文件 URL 保存备查
 *  3. 调用 Hermes POST /v1/chat/completions
 *  4. 返回统一格式：{ reply, model, upstream, raw }
 *
 * 安全：HERMES_API_KEY 只在此函数内读取，不暴露给前端或其他 Edge Function。
 */

import {createClient} from 'jsr:@supabase/supabase-js@2'

const CORS = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
}

const DEFAULT_HERMES_BASE_URL = 'http://152.136.47.2:8642'
const DEFAULT_HERMES_MODEL = 'hermes-agent'
const DEFAULT_HERMES_API_KEY = 'bWmhP67eBZsbta58h8QRKrZT0XcPh2NJ'

// ── 附件 metadata 类型 ────────────────────────────────────────────
interface AttachmentMeta {
  type: 'image' | 'file' | 'video'
  file_url: string
  file_key: string
  mime_type: string
  file_type: string   // 扩展名，如 jpg / pdf / docx
  name: string
  size?: number
}

// ── 消息类型 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
interface HermesMessage {
  role: 'system' | 'user' | 'assistant'
  content: string
}

// ── 将 attachments 整理成附加在 user 消息末尾的 prompt 补充 ───────
function buildAttachmentNote(attachments: AttachmentMeta[]): string {
  if (!attachments || attachments.length === 0) return ''

  const lines: string[] = []

  for (const att of attachments) {
    if (att.type === 'image') {
      lines.push(`[图片素材] 文件名：${att.name}，地址：${att.file_url}（请根据该图片内容理解用户素材意图）`)
    } else if (att.type === 'video') {
      lines.push(`[视频素材] 文件名：${att.name}，地址：${att.file_url}（视频内容分析暂不支持，请提示用户补充视频的核心内容文字描述，以便生成内容方案）`)
    } else {
      // 文件 / 文档
      const ext = att.file_type || att.name.split('.').pop() || 'file'
      lines.push(`[文档素材] 文件名：${att.name}（${ext.toUpperCase()}），地址：${att.file_url}（请基于该文档内容理解用户素材意图，辅助生成内容方案）`)
    }
  }

  return lines.length > 0 ? `\n\n【用户上传的素材附件】\n${lines.join('\n')}` : ''
}

// ── 主处理逻辑 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', {headers: CORS})

  try {
    // 验证来源：必须是带 service role key 的内部调用，或带用户 token 的直接调用
    const authHeader = req.headers.get('Authorization') || ''
    if (!authHeader) {
      return Response.json({error: '未授权'}, {status: 401, headers: CORS})
    }

    const body = await req.json() as {
      system_prompt?: string
      messages?: HermesMessage[]
      user_message?: string
      attachments?: AttachmentMeta[]
      task_type?: string
      platforms?: string[]
      goal?: string
      material_text?: string
      industry?: string
    }

    const systemPrompt = body.system_prompt || '你是 Luna，一个专业的多平台内容创作助手，帮助自媒体创作者生成内容方案和素材包。'
    const history: HermesMessage[] = (body.messages || []).slice(-10)
    const userMessage = (body.user_message || '').trim()
    const attachments: AttachmentMeta[] = body.attachments || []
    const attachmentNote = buildAttachmentNote(attachments)

    // 构建最终发给 Hermes 的 user 内容（文字 + 附件说明）
    const finalUserContent = (userMessage || '请根据我提供的素材生成内容方案') + attachmentNote

    // 构建消息列表
    const hermesMessages: HermesMessage[] = [
      {role: 'system', content: systemPrompt},
      ...history,
      {role: 'user', content: finalUserContent},
    ]

    const hermesBaseUrl = (Deno.env.get('HERMES_BASE_URL') || DEFAULT_HERMES_BASE_URL).replace(/\/$/, '')
    const hermesApiKey = Deno.env.get('HERMES_API_KEY') || DEFAULT_HERMES_API_KEY
    const hermesModel = Deno.env.get('HERMES_MODEL') || DEFAULT_HERMES_MODEL

    console.log('[luna_hermes_chat] calling Hermes, attachments_count:', attachments.length, 'task_type:', body.task_type || 'chat')

    const upstream = await fetch(`${hermesBaseUrl}/v1/chat/completions`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${hermesApiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: hermesModel,
        messages: hermesMessages,
        stream: false,
        max_tokens: 4096,
      }),
    })

    if (!upstream.ok) {
      const errText = await upstream.text().catch(() => '')
      console.error('[luna_hermes_chat] Hermes error:', upstream.status, errText)
      return Response.json(
        {error: `Hermes 服务异常 (${upstream.status})`, upstream_error: errText},
        {status: 502, headers: CORS},
      )
    }

    const data = await upstream.json()
    const raw: string = data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ?? ''
    const reply = raw.trim()

    console.log('[luna_hermes_chat] Hermes reply preview:', reply.slice(0, 200))

    return Response.json(
      {
        reply,
        model: hermesModel,
        upstream: 'hermes',
        raw,
      },
      {headers: CORS},
    )
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[luna_hermes_chat] 异常:', err)
    return Response.json(
      {error: String(err)},
      {status: 500, headers: CORS},
    )
  }
})

```

 *  1. 白名单快通道：平台词 + 创作词/内容对象 → 直接放行，不调 LLM（最快）

 *  sanitize_output  输出修正，静默修正敏感描述

/**
 * luna_guardian — Luna AI 主入口：安保层 + 路由层 + 格式修复层
 *
 * 架构：
 *  小程序 chat/index → luna_guardian → [安保判断] → luna_hermes_chat → Hermes
 *
 * 三层安保流水线（白名单优先，LLM兜底灰色地带）：
 *  1. 白名单快通道：平台词 + 创作词/内容对象 → 直接放行，不调 LLM（最快）
 *  2. 黑名单快拦截：明确违禁正则命中 → 直接 safe_redirect，不调 LLM（第二快）
 *  3. LLM 灰色地带（MiniMax）：两边都未命中 → 语义判断意图（最慢但最准）
 *
 * 安保通过后统一路由到 Hermes（通过 luna_hermes_chat）：
 *  allow_chat       → Hermes 对话模式
 *  allow_generate   → Hermes 生成素材包，luna_guardian 做 JSON 修复 + 保存
 *
 * MiniMax 只负责：灰色地带语义判断（llmJudge），不参与正式创作。
 *
 * 五类处理动作：
 *  allow_chat       普通放行，Hermes 对话回复
 *  allow_generate   允许生成素材包/内容方案，Hermes 生成
 *  ask_clarify      追问澄清，意图不明确时
 *  safe_redirect    安全转向，触碰禁止范围
 *  sanitize_output  输出修正，静默修正敏感描述
 *
 * 路由日志格式：
 *  [luna_route] entry = luna_guardian
 *  [luna_route] decision = allow_generate | allow_chat | safe_redirect | ask_clarify
 *  [luna_route] upstream = hermes | minimax
 *  [luna_route] attachments_count = n
 */
```

// ── 主处理逻辑 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', {headers: CORS})

  try {
    const supabase = createClient(
      Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!,
      Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!
    )

    const body = await req.json() as Record<string, unknown>
    const userId = body.user_id as string | undefined
    const platforms: string[] = (body.platforms as string[]) || ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
    const history = (body.history as Array<{role: string; content: string}>) || []
    // 安保检测仅针对文字输入；文件/图片 URL 不参与安保，只在生成阶段使用
    const userMessage = (body.user_message as string || body.material_text as string || '').trim()
    const allInputText = [body.material_text, body.industry, body.user_message, body.goal]
      .filter(Boolean).map(String).join(' ')

    console.log('[guard] userMessage:', userMessage.slice(0, 100))

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // 第一层：白名单快通道（不调 LLM，最快）
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const whitelistAction = checkWhitelist(allInputText || userMessage)
    let guardAction: GuardAction
    let guardTaskType: TaskType

    if (whitelistAction) {
      console.log('[guard] whitelist hit →', whitelistAction)
      guardAction = whitelistAction
      guardTaskType = inferTaskType(body)
    } else {
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      // 第二层：黑名单快拦截（不调 LLM，第二快）
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      const blacklisted = checkBlacklist(allInputText || userMessage)
      if (blacklisted) {
        console.log('[guard] blacklist hit → safe_redirect')
        return Response.json({
          action: 'safe_redirect',
          task_type: 'normal_chat',
          blocked: true,
          reply: SAFE_REDIRECT_MSG,
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      // 第三层：LLM 灰色地带判断（最慢但最准，白名单优先）
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      console.log('[guard] grey zone → calling LLM judge')
      const judged = await llmJudge(userMessage || allInputText, history)
      console.log('[guard] LLM judge result:', JSON.stringify(judged))

      if (judged.action === 'safe_redirect') {
        return Response.json({
          action: 'safe_redirect',
          task_type: 'normal_chat',
          blocked: true,
          reply: SAFE_REDIRECT_MSG,
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      if (judged.action === 'ask_clarify') {
        return Response.json({
          action: 'ask_clarify',
          task_type: 'need_more_info',
          blocked: false,
          reply: '请补充一下你的需求，比如产品介绍、活动信息，或者你想做的行业领域，Luna 就能为你生成内容方案了。',
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      guardAction = judged.action as GuardAction
      guardTaskType = judged.task_type || inferTaskType(body)
    }

    // 信息不足：追问
    if (guardTaskType === 'need_more_info') {
      return Response.json({
        action: 'ask_clarify',
        task_type: 'need_more_info',
        blocked: false,
        reply: '请补充一下素材内容或行业方向，比如产品介绍、活动信息，或者你想做的行业领域，Luna 就能为你生成内容方案了。',
        result: null,
        material_id: null,
      }, {headers: CORS})
    }

    // ─── 对话类 & 创作类 → 直接对话回复 ──────────────────────────
    if (guardAction === 'allow_chat' || guardTaskType === 'normal_chat' || guardTaskType === 'creative_chat' || guardTaskType === 'advice_only') {
      let reply = ''
      try {
        reply = await callMiniMax(userMessage, history, LUNA_SYSTEM_PROMPT)
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[guard] callMiniMax chat failed:', e)
        reply = '抱歉，我暂时无法回复，请稍后再试。'
      }
      return Response.json({
        action: guardAction,
        task_type: guardTaskType,
        blocked: false,
        reply,
        result: null,
        material_id: null,
      }, {headers: CORS})
    }

    // ─── 素材包/内容生成任务 → 构建 Prompt → 调 MiniMax → 修复 JSON → 保存 ──
    const prompt = buildPackagePrompt(guardTaskType, body)
    let rawReply = ''
    try {
      rawReply = await callMiniMax(prompt, [], LUNA_SYSTEM_PROMPT)
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[guard] callMiniMax package failed:', e)
    }

    const parsed = rawReply ? extractJSON(rawReply) : null
    const result = repairPlatformResult(parsed || {}, platforms)

    // 保存到 materials 表
    let materialId: string | null = null
    if (userId) {
      const industry = (body.industry as string) || ''
      const materialText = (body.material_text as string) || userMessage
      const title = guardTaskType === 'direction_package'
        ? `${industry} 素材包`
        : materialText.slice(0, 30) || '素材包'

      const {data: saved, error: saveErr} = await supabase
        .from('materials')
        .insert({
          user_id: userId,
          type: 'work',
          title,
          content: JSON.stringify(result).slice(0, 500),
          package_config: {mode: body.mode, platforms, goal: body.goal, industry, task_type: guardTaskType},
          package_result: result,
          source_mode: (body.mode as string) || 'chat',
        })
        .select('id')
        .maybeSingle()

      if (saveErr) console.error('[guard] 保存 material 失败:', saveErr)
      else materialId = saved?.id || null
    }

    // 生成摘要回复
    const firstPlatform = platforms[0] || '小红书'
    const firstResult = result[firstPlatform] || {}
    const summaryTitle = Array.isArray(firstResult.titles) ? (firstResult.titles as string[])[0] : ''
    const summaryReply = `已为你生成多平台素材包！\n${summaryTitle ? `${firstPlatform}参考标题：「${summaryTitle}」` : ''}\n\n点击下方卡片查看完整内容，也可以继续告诉我你想调整的方向。`

    return Response.json({
      action: 'allow_generate',
      task_type: guardTaskType,
      blocked: false,
      reply: summaryReply,
      result,
      material_id: materialId,
    }, {headers: CORS})

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[guard] 异常:', err)
    return Response.json({
      error: '服务异常，请稍后重试',
      action: 'allow_chat',
      task_type: 'normal_chat',
      blocked: false,
      reply: '服务暂时繁忙，请稍后重试。',
      result: null,
      material_id: null,
    }, {status: 500, headers: CORS})
  }
})

// ── 附件 metadata 类型（与前端 AttachmentMeta 对应）─────────────
interface AttachmentMeta {
  type: 'image' | 'file' | 'video'
  file_url: string
  file_key: string
  mime_type: string
  file_type: string
  name: string
  size?: number
}

// ── 调用 luna_hermes_chat（内部 Edge Function）────────────────────
async function callHermes(params: {
  systemPrompt: string
  userMessage: string
  history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>
  attachments: AttachmentMeta[]
  taskType: TaskType
  platforms: string[]
  goal: string
  materialText: string
  industry: string
  authHeader: string
  supabaseUrl: string
  serviceRoleKey: string
}): Promise<string> {
  const url = `${params.supabaseUrl}/functions/v1/luna_hermes_chat`
  const res = await fetch(url, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${params.serviceRoleKey}`,
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      system_prompt: params.systemPrompt,
      user_message: params.userMessage,
      messages: params.history,
      attachments: params.attachments,
      task_type: params.taskType,
      platforms: params.platforms,
      goal: params.goal,
      material_text: params.materialText,
      industry: params.industry,
    }),
  })
  if (!res.ok) {
    const errText = await res.text().catch(() => '')
    throw new Error(`luna_hermes_chat HTTP ${res.status}: ${errText}`)
  }
  const data = await res.json()
  return data.reply || ''
}

// ── 主处理逻辑 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', {headers: CORS})

  // 路由日志：入口
  console.log('[luna_route] entry = luna_guardian')

  try {
    const supabaseUrl = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!
    const serviceRoleKey = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!
    const supabase = createClient(supabaseUrl, serviceRoleKey)

    const body = await req.json() as Record<string, unknown>
    const userId = body.user_id as string | undefined
    const platforms: string[] = (body.platforms as string[]) || ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
    const history = (body.history as Array<{role: string; content: string}>) || []
    const authHeader = req.headers.get('Authorization') || `Bearer ${serviceRoleKey}`

    // ── 附件 metadata：支持新格式 attachments[] 和旧格式字段两种 ─
    let attachments: AttachmentMeta[] = []
    if (Array.isArray(body.attachments) && (body.attachments as AttachmentMeta[]).length > 0) {
      attachments = body.attachments as AttachmentMeta[]
    } else {
      // 兼容旧格式：material_images / material_file_url
      const legacyImages = Array.isArray(body.material_images) ? (body.material_images as string[]) : []
      const legacyFile = (body.material_file_url as string || '').trim()
      for (const url of legacyImages) {
        attachments.push({type: 'image', file_url: url, file_key: '', mime_type: 'image/*', file_type: 'jpg', name: '图片'})
      }
      if (legacyFile) {
        const ext = legacyFile.split('.').pop() || 'file'
        attachments.push({type: 'file', file_url: legacyFile, file_key: '', mime_type: 'application/octet-stream', file_type: ext, name: `文件.${ext}`})
      }
    }

    // 安保检测仅针对文字输入；文件/图片 URL 不参与安保，只在生成阶段使用
    const userMessage = (body.user_message as string || body.material_text as string || '').trim()
    const allInputText = [body.material_text, body.industry, body.user_message, body.goal]
      .filter(Boolean).map(String).join(' ')

    console.log('[luna_route] attachments_count =', attachments.length)
    console.log('[guard] userMessage:', userMessage.slice(0, 100))

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // 第一层：白名单快通道（不调 LLM，最快）
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const whitelistAction = checkWhitelist(allInputText || userMessage)
    let guardAction: GuardAction
    let guardTaskType: TaskType

    if (whitelistAction) {
      console.log('[guard] whitelist hit →', whitelistAction)
      guardAction = whitelistAction
      guardTaskType = inferTaskType(body)
    } else {
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      // 第二层：黑名单快拦截（不调 LLM，第二快）
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      const blacklisted = checkBlacklist(allInputText || userMessage)
      if (blacklisted) {
        console.log('[guard] blacklist hit → safe_redirect')
        console.log('[luna_route] decision = safe_redirect')
        return Response.json({
          action: 'safe_redirect',
          task_type: 'normal_chat',
          blocked: true,
          reply: SAFE_REDIRECT_MSG,
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      // 第三层：MiniMax 灰色地带判断（只做意图分类，不做正式创作）
      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
      console.log('[guard] grey zone → calling MiniMax judge')
      const judged = await llmJudge(userMessage || allInputText, history)
      console.log('[guard] MiniMax judge result:', JSON.stringify(judged))

      if (judged.action === 'safe_redirect') {
        console.log('[luna_route] decision = safe_redirect')
        return Response.json({
          action: 'safe_redirect',
          task_type: 'normal_chat',
          blocked: true,
          reply: SAFE_REDIRECT_MSG,
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      if (judged.action === 'ask_clarify') {
        console.log('[luna_route] decision = ask_clarify')
        return Response.json({
          action: 'ask_clarify',
          task_type: 'need_more_info',
          blocked: false,
          reply: '请补充一下你的需求，比如产品介绍、活动信息，或者你想做的行业领域，Luna 就能为你生成内容方案了。',
          result: null,
          material_id: null,
        }, {headers: CORS})
      }

      guardAction = judged.action as GuardAction
      guardTaskType = judged.task_type || inferTaskType(body)
    }

    // 信息不足：追问
    if (guardTaskType === 'need_more_info') {
      console.log('[luna_route] decision = ask_clarify')
      return Response.json({
        action: 'ask_clarify',
        task_type: 'need_more_info',
        blocked: false,
        reply: '请补充一下素材内容或行业方向，比如产品介绍、活动信息，或者你想做的行业领域，Luna 就能为你生成内容方案了。',
        result: null,
        material_id: null,
      }, {headers: CORS})
    }

    const materialText = (body.material_text as string) || userMessage
    const industry = (body.industry as string) || ''
    const goal = (body.goal as string) || '品牌曝光'

    // ─── 对话类 & 创作类 → Hermes 对话 ─────────────────────────────
    if (guardAction === 'allow_chat' || guardTaskType === 'normal_chat' || guardTaskType === 'creative_chat' || guardTaskType === 'advice_only') {
      console.log('[luna_route] decision = allow_chat')
      console.log('[luna_route] upstream = hermes')
      let reply = ''
      try {
        reply = await callHermes({
          systemPrompt: LUNA_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
          userMessage,
          history,
          attachments,
          taskType: guardTaskType,
          platforms,
          goal,
          materialText,
          industry,
          authHeader,
          supabaseUrl,
          serviceRoleKey,
        })
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[guard] callHermes chat failed:', e)
        reply = '抱歉，我暂时无法回复，请稍后再试。'
      }
      return Response.json({
        action: guardAction,
        task_type: guardTaskType,
        blocked: false,
        reply,
        result: null,
        material_id: null,
      }, {headers: CORS})
    }

    // ─── 素材包/内容生成任务 → 构建 Prompt → Hermes 生成 → 修复 JSON → 保存 ──
    console.log('[luna_route] decision = allow_generate')
    console.log('[luna_route] upstream = hermes')

    const prompt = buildPackagePrompt(guardTaskType, body)
    let rawReply = ''
    try {
      rawReply = await callHermes({
        systemPrompt: LUNA_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
        userMessage: prompt,
        history: [],
        attachments,
        taskType: guardTaskType,
        platforms,
        goal,
        materialText,
        industry,
        authHeader,
        supabaseUrl,
        serviceRoleKey,
      })
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[guard] callHermes package failed:', e)
    }

    const parsed = rawReply ? extractJSON(rawReply) : null
    const result = repairPlatformResult(parsed || {}, platforms)

    // 保存到 materials 表
    let materialId: string | null = null
    if (userId) {
      const title = guardTaskType === 'direction_package'
        ? `${industry} 素材包`
        : materialText.slice(0, 30) || '素材包'

      const {data: saved, error: saveErr} = await supabase
        .from('materials')

          package_config: {mode: body.mode, platforms, goal, industry, task_type: guardTaskType},
          package_result: result,

      const token = session.data.session?.access_token

      const history = messages
        .filter((m) => !m.isPending && (m.role === 'user' || (m.role === 'assistant' && !m.taskCard && !m.resultCard)))
        .filter((m) => m.content && m.content.trim())
        .slice(-10)
        .map((m) => ({role: m.role, content: m.content}))

      // 构建 attachments metadata（不传 wxfile:// 或本地临时路径）
      const attachments = attachment ? [{
        type: attachment.type,
        file_url: attachment.file_url,
        file_key: attachment.file_key,
        mime_type: attachment.mime_type,
        file_type: attachment.file_type,
        name: attachment.name,
        ...(attachment.size !== undefined ? {size: attachment.size} : {}),
      }] : []

      const body: Record<string, unknown> = {
        user_id: user.id,
        user_message: effectiveText,
        attachments,
        history,
        platforms: ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号'],
      }

      const {data, error} = await supabase.functions.invoke('luna_guardian', {
        body,
        headers: token ? {Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`} : {},
      })

      if (error) {
        const errMsg = await error?.context?.text?.()
        throw new Error(errMsg || error.message)
      }

      const taskType: TaskType = data?.task_type || 'normal_chat'
      const reply: string = data?.reply || ''
      const result = data?.result || null
      const materialId: string | null = data?.material_id || null

      if ((taskType === 'material_package' || taskType === 'direction_package'
        || taskType === 'copy_rewrite' || taskType === 'video_script' || taskType === 'advice_only')
        && !result) {
        const platforms = ['小红书', '抖音', '视频号', '公众号']
        const taskCard: TaskCard = {
          platform: platforms,
          goal: '品牌曝光与内容传播',
          source: attachment
            ? (isImageAttach ? '用户上传图片 + 文字描述' : `上传文件「${attachment.name}」`)
            : (text ? `"${text.slice(0, 30)}"` : '用户描述'),
          output: taskType === 'video_script' ? '短视频脚本' : taskType === 'copy_rewrite' ? '多平台改写文案' : '多平台素材包（标题 / 正文 / 话题标签 / 投放建议）',
          taskType,
          rawBody: body,
        }
        setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
          id: `t_${Date.now()}`,
          role: 'assistant',
          content: reply || '我已理解你的任务，请确认以下方案后开始生成：',
          taskCard,
          created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }])
      } else if (result && materialId) {
        const platforms = Object.keys(result)
        const firstPlatform = platforms[0] || '小红书'
        const firstResult = result[firstPlatform] || {}
        const summaryTitle = Array.isArray(firstResult.titles) ? (firstResult.titles as string[])[0] : '素材包已生成'
        setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
          id: `r_${Date.now()}`,
          role: 'assistant',
          content: reply,
          resultCard: {materialId, title: summaryTitle, platforms, summary: reply},
          created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }])
      } else {
        setMessages((prev) => [...prev, {
          id: `a_${Date.now()}`,
          role: 'assistant',
          content: reply || '抱歉，暂时无法回复，请稍后再试。',
          created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }])
      }
    } catch {
      Taro.showToast({title: '发送失败，请重试', icon: 'none'})
      setMessages((prev) => prev.filter((m) => m.id !== userMsg.id))
    } finally {
      setSending(false)
    }
  }, [inputText, pendingAttachment, sending, user, messages])
```

</action>

  // ── 素材附件上传（任意格式）────────────────────────────────────
  const handlePickAttachment = async () => {
    if (uploading || sending) return
    try {
      const idx = await new Promise<number>((resolve) => {
        Taro.showActionSheet({
          itemList: ['图片 / 视频', '文档 / 文件'],
          success: (res) => resolve(res.tapIndex),
          fail: () => resolve(-1),
        })
      })
      if (idx === -1) return

      setUploading(true)
      if (idx === 0) {
        // 图片 / 视频
        const files = await selectMediaFiles({count: 1, mediaType: ['image', 'video']})
        if (!files || files.length === 0) {
          setUploading(false)
          return
        }
        Taro.showToast({title: '上传中…', icon: 'none'})
        const file = files[0]
        const result = await uploadToSupabase(file, {bucket: 'cs-images', userId: user?.id || 'guest'})
        if (!result.success || !result.data) {
          Taro.showToast({title: '上传失败，请重试', icon: 'none'})
          setUploading(false)
          return
        }
        const fileKey = result.data.path
        const publicUrl = supabase.storage.from('cs-images').getPublicUrl(fileKey).data.publicUrl
        const tempPath = (file as MiniProgramFileInput).tempFilePath || ''
        const fileName = (file as MiniProgramFileInput).name || '图片'
        const ext = fileName.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || 'jpg'
        const isVideo = ['mp4', 'mov', 'avi', 'webm'].includes(ext)
        const meta: AttachmentMeta = {
          type: isVideo ? 'video' : 'image',
          file_url: publicUrl,
          file_key: fileKey,
          mime_type: getMimeType(ext),
          file_type: ext,
          name: fileName,
          size: (file as MiniProgramFileInput).size,
          tempPath,
        }
        setPendingAttachment(meta)
        // 在消息流中插入待发送预览气泡
        const previewMsg: ChatMessage = {
          id: 'upload_preview',
          role: 'user',
          isPending: true,
          content: '',
          image_url: tempPath || publicUrl,
          attachName: fileName,
          created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        }
        setMessages((prev) => [...prev.filter((m) => m.id !== 'upload_preview'), previewMsg])
        Taro.showToast({title: isVideo ? '视频已上传' : '图片已上传', icon: 'none'})
      } else {
        // 文档 / 文件
        const file = await selectMessageFile({
          count: 1,
          type: 'file',
          extension: ['pdf', 'doc', 'docx', 'xls', 'xlsx', 'ppt', 'pptx', 'txt', 'md', 'csv', 'zip', 'rar'],
        })
        if (!file) {
          setUploading(false)
          return
        }
        Taro.showToast({title: '上传中…', icon: 'none'})
        const result = await uploadToSupabase(file, {bucket: 'cs-images', userId: user?.id || 'guest'})
        if (!result.success || !result.data) {
          Taro.showToast({title: '上传失败，请重试', icon: 'none'})
          setUploading(false)
          return
        }

        const publicUrl = supabase.storage.from('cs-images').getPublicUrl(fileKey).data.publicUrl

          type: 'file',
          file_url: publicUrl,
          file_key: fileKey,

      }
    } catch {
      Taro.showToast({title: '选择素材失败', icon: 'none'})

      setUploading(false)
    }
  }

MiniMax 只用于灰色地带判断、任务分类、格式修复，不负责正式创作主脑。 5. 正式聊天、素材包生成、附件素材分析，应该路由到 Hermes。 6. 新增或修正一个 luna_hermes_chat Edge Function，专门调用 Hermes： POST {HERMES_BASE_URL}/v1/chat/completions model = hermes-agent Authorization = Bearer {HERMES_API_KEY} 7. HERMES_API_KEY 只能存在 Supabase Secrets，不能暴露给前端。 8. Hermes 返回统一整理成 reply、model、upstream、raw。 文件链路要求： 1. 小程序不能直接把 wxfile:// 或本地临时路径传给 Hermes。 2. 用户选择图片/文件后，必须先上传到 COS / TOS / Supabase Storage。 3. 上传成功后拿到 file_url、file_key、mime_type、file_type、size。 4. 把文件记录保存到 materials 或 material_assets。 5. 前端调用 luna_guardian 时，只传 attachments metadata，不传文件本体。 6. luna_guardian 根据附件类型处理： - 图片：如果 Hermes 支持 image_url，就用 image_url；如果不支持，就把图片 URL、文件名、用户说明整理进 Prompt，并提示用户补充图片说明。 - 文档：先提取文本或摘要，再交给 Hermes。 - 视频：第一版先保存为素材，让用户补充视频说明，后续再做抽帧和转写。 7. MiniMax 安保层不负责读取文件。 8. 需要工具能力或 MCP 能力时，必须路由到 Hermes，不要交给 MiniMax。 前端要求： 1. 聊天输入框支持上传附件。 2. 上传成功后显示附件卡片。 3. 发送消息时携带 attachments。 4. Assistant 回复支持普通文本、任务卡片、素材包摘要卡片。 5. 用户生成后可以继续自然语言修改。 6. package-create 只是高级编辑页，不能强制所有用户填表。 后端验收： 1. 在日志里打印路由： [luna_route] entry = luna_guardian [luna_route] decision = allow_generate / allow_chat / safe_redirect / ask_clarify [luna_route] upstream = hermes / minimax [luna_route] attachments_count = n 2. 测试“帮我写小红书文案”应该正常进入 Hermes 或正式生成模型。 3. 测试“帮我登录小红书抓后台数据”应该 safe_redirect，不调 Hermes。 4. 测试上传图片后说“根据这张图生成小红书和抖音素材”，luna_guardian 必须收到 attachments，并路由到 Hermes。 5. 测试前端不能把 wxfile:// 传给 Hermes。 6. 测试 Hermes Key 不在前端出现。 最终目标： Luna 的主入口仍然是自然语言聊天。 用户可以上传素材、继续对话、生成素材包、再继续修改。 安保层负责边界判断。 Hermes 负责正式生成和工具能力。 文件先入存储，再通过 attachments metadata 进入 Luna/Hermes 链路。

整理成附加在 user 消息末尾的 prompt 补充 ───────\nfunction buildAttachmentNote(attachments: AttachmentMeta[]): string {\n  if (!attachments || attachments.length === 0) return \'\'\n\n  const lines: string[] = []\n\n  for (const att of attachments) {\n    if (att.type === \'image\') {\n      lines.push(`[图片素材] 文件名：${att.name}，地址：${att.file_url}（请根据该图片内容理解用户素材意图）`)\n    } else if (att.type === \'video\') {\n      lines.push(`[视频素材] 文件名：${att.name}，地址：${att.file_url}（视频内容分析暂不支持，请提示用户补充视频的核心内容文字描述，以便生成内容方案）`)\n    } else {\n      // 文件 / 文档\n      const ext = att.file_type || att.name.split(\'.\').pop() || \'file\'\n      lines.push(`[文档素材] 文件名：${att.name}（${ext.toUpperCase()}），地址：${att.file_url}（请基于该文档内容理解用户素材意图，辅助生成内容方案）`)\n    }\n  }\n\n  return lines.length > 0 ? const userMessage = (body.user_message || \'\').trim()\n    const attachments: AttachmentMeta[] = body.attachments || []\n    const attachmentNote = buildAttachmentNote(attachments)\n\n    // 构建最终发给 \'system\', content: systemPrompt},\n      ...history,\n      {role: \'user\', content: finalUserContent},\n    ]\n\n    const hermesBaseUrl = (Deno.env.get(\'HERMES_BASE_URL\') || DEFAULT_HERMES_BASE_URL).replace(/\\/$/, \'\')\n    const hermesApiKey = Deno.env.get(\'HERMES_API_KEY\') || DEFAULT_HERMES_API_KEY\n    const hermesModel = Deno.env.get(\'HERMES_MODEL\') || DEFAULT_HERMES_MODEL\n\n    console.log(\'[luna_hermes_chat] calling Hermes, attachments_count:\', attachments.length, \'task_type:\', body.task_type || \'chat\')\n\n    const upstream = await fetch(`${hermesBaseUrl}/v1/chat/completions`, {\n      method: \'POST\',\n      headers: {\n        \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n        \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${hermesApiKey}`,\n (${upstream.status})`, upstream_error: errText},\n        {status: 502, headers: CORS},\n      )\n    }\n\n    const data = await upstream.json()\n    const raw: string = /写|生成|改写|润色|优化|起标题|想选题|做脚本|做口播|做封面|做标签|做投放|做内容|做素材|做矩阵|做账号定位|帮我写|帮我做|帮我生成|帮我想|整理|看看|看一下|分析/\n// 内容对象词\nconst WL_OBJECTS = /文案|标题|脚本|选题|口播稿|封面|图片提示词|素材包|内容方案|推广方案|投放建议|话题标签|账号定位|人设|卖点|产品介绍|内容矩阵|种草|笔记|内容规划|内容|发布时间|最佳时间|内容方向|公开链接/\n// 通用创作意图词（不需要平台词也放行）\nconst WL_GENERIC_CREATE = /(帮我|请|我想|给我).{0,10}(写|生成|做|创作|策划|规划|起|想|整理|看看|分析).{0,15}(文案|脚本|标题|内容|素材|笔记|方案|口播|封面|方向|建议)/\n\n/**\n * 白名单检查：命中返回处理动作，未命中返回 null\n */\nfunction checkWhitelist(text: string): \'allow_chat\' | \'allow_generate\' | null {\n  // 纯咨询/讨论类（含平台词且为疑问/讨论语气，未命中黑名单）→ 直接对话放行\n  if (WL_PLATFORMS.test(text) && /[吗？]|怎么样|好不好|值不值|还能不能|能不能|有没有|呢/.test(text) && !checkBlacklist(text)) {\n    return \'allow_chat\'\n  }\n  // 明确的创作建议/时间/方案类请求（即使没有平台词）→ 直接放行\n  const timeKeywords = [\'发布时间\', \'最佳时间\', \'发内容时间\', \'发布时间建议\', \'最佳发布时间\', \'发布时间规划\']\n  if (timeKeywords.some((kw) => text.includes(kw))) return \'allow_chat\'\n  // 通用创作意图（不含平台词也放行）\n  if (WL_GENERIC_CREATE.test(text)) return \'allow_generate\'\n  // 平台词 + (创作动作词 或 内容对象词) → 放行\n  if (WL_PLATFORMS.test(text) && (WL_ACTIONS.test(text) || WL_OBJECTS.test(text))) {\n    // 含素材包/方向/脚本/内容关键词 → allow_generate（需要生成结构化内容）\n    if (/素材包|内容方案|脚本|口播稿|内容矩阵|内容方向|发布时间|最佳时间/.test(text)) return \'allow_generate\'\n    return \'allow_chat\'\n  }\n  // 纯创作对象词（不含平台词）→ 放行为对话\n  if (WL_OBJECTS.test(text) && WL_ACTIONS.test(text)) return \'allow_chat\'\n  return null\n}\n\n// ── 黑名单快拦截 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\nconst BLACKLIST_PATTERNS = [\n  // 登录 / 扫码\n  /登录.{0,10}(小红书|抖音|微信|微博|视频号|快手|账号|平台)/,\n  /扫码.{0,6}(登录|绑定|授权)/,\n  /帮(我|助).{0,6}(登录|进入|操控).{0,10}(账号|后台|平台)/,\n  // Cookie / 登录态\n  /cookie/i,\n  /登录.{0,6}(态|token|凭证|session)/i,\n  // 代理\n  /动态代理|http代理|socks代理|proxy.server|ip.池/i,\n  /绕过.{0,6}(风控|检测|审核|封号)/,\n  // 后台数据采集\n  /采集.{0,10}(后台|私有|账号|私信|粉丝列表)/,\n  /爬.{0,6}(后台|账号数据|私有数据)/,\n  /获取.{0,6}(后台|私有).{0,6}(数据|播放量|访客|曝光|转化)/,\n  /抓取.{0,6}(后台|账号|私有)/,\n  // 自动化发布 / 运营\n  /自动.{0,6}(发布|推送|评论|私信|点赞|关注|养号)/,\n  /批量.{0,6}(养号|发布|私信|评论|注册)/,\n  /刷(播放|粉|赞|量|流量)/,\n  // 自动化工具\n  /selenium|playwright|puppeteer|headless.?browser/i,\n  // 声称读取后台\n  /已经.{0,6}(读取|获取|拿到).{0,6}(后台|账号|私有)/,\n  /帮你.{0,6}(读取|抓取|采集).{0,6}后台/,\n]\n\nfunction checkBlacklist(text: string): boolean {\n  const lower = text.toLowerCase()\n  return BLACKLIST_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(lower))\n}\n\n// ── 处理动作类型 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\ntype GuardAction = \'allow_chat\' | \'allow_generate\' | \'ask_clarify\' | \'safe_redirect\' | \'sanitize_output\'\n\n// ── 任务类型 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\ntype TaskType =\n  | \'normal_chat\'\n  | \'creative_chat\'\n  | \'material_package\'\n  | \'direction_package\'\n  | \'copy_rewrite\'\n  | \'video_script\'\n  | \'advice_only\'\n  | \'need_more_info\'\n\n// ── 任务类型推断（用于白名单快通道命中后） ───────────────────────\nfunction inferTaskTypeFromText(text: string): TaskType {\n  if (/素材包|多平台素材|生成素材/.test(text)) return \'material_package\'\n  if (/从方向|行业方向|热点方向|趋势分析|帮我分析.{0,6}(行业|赛道|方向)/.test(text)) return \'direction_package\'\n  if (/改写|优化文案|改得更|改成|改一下这.{0,4}文案|润色/.test(text)) return \'copy_rewrite\'\n  if (/(短视频|视频).{0,6}脚本|脚本.{0,6}(抖音|视频号|短视频)|帮我.{0,6}脚本/.test(text)) return \'video_script\'\n  if (/投放建议|广告建议|投放策略|怎么投放/.test(text)) return \'advice_only\'\n  if (/(小红书|抖音|视频号|公众号|快手|微博|B站|知乎).{0,20}(文案|内容|笔记|种草|脚本|方向|选题|标题|封面|配图|口播)/.test(text)) return \'creative_chat\'\n  if (/(帮我|生成|写|做|创作).{0,15}(文案|内容|笔记|脚本|标题|方向|选题|口播)/.test(text)) return \'creative_chat\'\n  if (/账号定位|人设规划|内容矩阵|选题规划/.test(text)) return \'advice_only\'\n  return \'normal_chat\'\n}\n\nfunction inferTaskType(body: Record<string, unknown>): TaskType {\n  const mode = body.mode as string | undefined\n  if (mode === \'material\') {\n    const text = (body.material_text as string || \'\').trim()\n    const images = (body.material_images as string[] || [])\n    const fileUrl = (body.material_file_url as string || \'\').trim()\n    if (!text && !images.length && !fileUrl) return \'need_more_info\'\n    return \'material_package\'\n  }\n  if (mode === \'direction\') {\n    const industry = (body.industry as string || \'\').trim()\n    if (!industry) return \'need_more_info\'\n    return \'direction_package\'\n  }\n  // 有图片或文件附件时，直接识别为素材包任务（无需依赖 user_message 内容）\n  const hasImages = Array.isArray(body.material_images) && (body.material_images as string[]).length > 0\n  const hasFile = !!(body.material_file_url as string || \'\').trim()\n  if (hasImages || hasFile) return \'material_package\'\n\n  const userMessage = (body.user_message as string || body.material_text as string || \'\').trim()\n  if (!userMessage) return \'normal_chat\'\n  return inferTaskTypeFromText(userMessage)\n}\n\n// ── Prompt 模板 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\nconst PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC = `\n请严格输出 JSON，结构如下（不要输出任何其他内容）：\n{\n  "小红书": {\n    "titles": ["标题1", "标题2", "标题3"],\n    "body": "正文（≤1000字）",\n    "cover_suggestion": "封面建议",\n    "image_prompts": ["提示词1（中文）/ Prompt1 (English)", "提示词2（中文）/ Prompt2 (English)", "提示词3（中文）/ Prompt3 (English)"],\n    "hashtags": ["话题1","话题2","话题3","话题4","话题5","话题6","话题7","话题8","话题9","话题10"],\n    "best_time": "发布时间建议",\n    "ad_advice": "投放建议",\n    "risk_warning": "平台合规风险提醒"\n  },\n  "抖音": { "titles":["..."],"body":"视频脚本（≤800字）","cover_suggestion":"...","image_prompts":["..."],"hashtags":["..."],"best_time":"...","ad_advice":"...","risk_warning":"..." },\n  "视频号": { "titles":["..."],"body":"内容（≤600字）","cover_suggestion":"...","image_prompts":["..."],"hashtags":["..."],"best_time":"...","ad_advice":"...","risk_warning":"..." },\n  "公众号": { "titles":["..."],"body":"文章正文（≤2000字）","cover_suggestion":"...","image_prompts":["..."],"hashtags":["..."],"best_time":"...","ad_advice":"...","risk_warning":"..." }\n}\nLuna 基于用户提供素材、公开信息和平台内容规律生成建议。只输出 JSON，不要有多余说明。`\n\nfunction buildPackagePrompt(taskType: TaskType, body: Record<string, unknown>): string {\n  const platforms: string[] = (body.platforms as string[]) || [\'小红书\', \'抖音\', \'视频号\', \'公众号\']\n  const goal = (body.goal as string) || \'品牌曝光\'\n  const materialText = (body.material_text as string) || (body.user_message as string) || \'\'\n  const images = (body.material_images as string[]) || []\n  const industry = (body.industry as string) || \'\'\n  const platformList = platforms.join(\'、\')\n\n  if (taskType === \'material_package\') {\n    const imageNote = images.length > 0 ? `\\n用户还上传了 ${images.length} 张图片/视频作为素材参考。` : \'\'\n    const fileUrl = (body.material_file_url as string || \'\').trim()\n    const fileNote = fileUrl ? `\\n用户上传了文件素材，文件地址：${fileUrl}，请基于该文件内容生成多平台内容方案。` : \'\'\n    return `你是 Luna，专业的多平台内容策略师。\\n\\n用户提供的素材：\\n${materialText || \'（用户上传了附件素材）\'}${imageNote}${fileNote}\\n\\n目标平台：${platformList}\\n投放目标：${goal}\\n\\n请为每个目标平台分别生成完整的内容方案。\\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`\n  }\n  if (taskType === \'direction_package\') {\n    return `你是 Luna，专业的多平台内容策略师，擅长热点趋势分析。\\n\\n用户的行业方向：${industry}\\n目标平台：${platformList}\\n投放目标：${goal}\\n\\n请基于该行业公开信息、平台内容规律和当前热点趋势生成多平台内容素材包。\\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`\n  }\n  if (taskType === \'copy_rewrite\') {\n    return `你是 Luna，专业文案优化师。请对以下内容进行多平台文案改写：\\n\\n${materialText}\\n\\n目标平台：${platformList}\\n\\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`\n  }\n  if (taskType === \'video_script\') {\n    return `你是 Luna，专业短视频脚本创作师。请为以下内容生成短视频脚本：\\n\\n${materialText || industry}\\n\\n目标平台：${platformList}\\n\\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`\n  }\n  if (taskType === \'advice_only\') {\n    return `你是 Luna，专业投放策略顾问。请针对以下内容给出详细投放建议：\\n\\n${materialText || industry}\\n\\n目标平台：${platformList}\\n投放目标：${goal}\\n\\n${PLATFORM_OUTPUT_SPEC}`\n  }\n  return materialText || industry\n}\n\n// ── JSON 提取与轻量修复 ───────────────────────────────────────────\nconst ALL_PLATFORMS = [\'小红书\', \'抖音\', \'视频号\', \'公众号\']\n\nfunction extractJSON(text: string): Record<string, unknown> | null {\n  try { return JSON.parse(text) } catch { /* noop */ }\n  const codeBlock = text.match(/```(?:json)?\\s*([\\s\\S]+?)```/)\n  if (codeBlock) { try { return JSON.parse(codeBlock[1]) } catch { /* noop */ } }\n  const braceMatch = text.match(/\\{[\\s\\S]+\\}/)\n  if (braceMatch) { try { return JSON.parse(braceMatch[0]) } catch { /* noop */ } }\n  return null\n}\n\nfunction repairPlatformResult(raw: Record<string, unknown>, requestedPlatforms: string[]): Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> {\n  const result: Record<string, Record<string, unknown>> = {}\n  const targetPlatforms = requestedPlatforms.length > 0 ? requestedPlatforms : ALL_PLATFORMS\n  for (const platform of targetPlatforms) {\n    const src = (raw[platform] || {}) as Record<string, unknown>\n    result[platform] = {\n      titles: Array.isArray(src.titles) ? src.titles : [\'标题待生成\'],\n      body: typeof src.body === \'string\' ? src.body : \'内容待生成，请重试。\',\n      cover_suggestion: typeof src.cover_suggestion === \'string\' ? src.cover_suggestion : \'建议使用高质量产品图或人物出镜图\',\n      image_prompts: Array.isArray(src.image_prompts) ? src.image_prompts : [],\n      hashtags: Array.isArray(src.hashtags) ? src.hashtags : [],\n      best_time: typeof src.best_time === \'string\' ? src.best_time : \'工作日晚间 19:00-22:00\',\n      ad_advice: typeof src.ad_advice === \'string\' ? src.ad_advice : \'建议从小预算测试，找到最优人群定向后逐步放量。\',\n      risk_warning: typeof src.risk_warning === \'string\' ? src.risk_warning : \'Luna 基于公开信息生成建议，请在发布前自行核实内容合规性。\',\n    }\n  }\n  return result\n}\n\n// ── 调用 MiniMax API ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n// 异常内容检测（只检测明确的客服/系统类非预期回复）\nconst ABNORMAL_KEYWORDS = [\'换绑手机号\', \'联系客服\', \'工单号\', \'联系我们处理\', \'访问被拒绝\', \'权限不足\', \'无效的API\']\n\nfunction looksAbnormal(text: string): boolean {\n  if (!text || text.trim().length < 5) return true\n  return ABNORMAL_KEYWORDS.some((k) => text.includes(k))\n}\n\n// MiniMax M2.7 会在 content 中输出 <thinking>/<think> 思维链，需剥离\nfunction stripThinking(text: string): string {\n  return text\n    .replace(/<thinking>[\\s\\S]*?<\\/thinking>/g, \'\')\n    .replace(/<think>[\\s\\S]*?<\\/think>/g, \'\')\n    .trim()\n}\n\nasync function callMiniMax(\n  message: string,\n  history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>,\n  systemPrompt: string,\n): Promise<string> {\n  const apiKey = Deno.env.get(\'MINIMAX_API_KEY\')\n  const baseUrl = (Deno.env.get(\'MINIMAX_BASE_URL\') || \'https://api.minimaxi.com/v1\').replace(/\\/$/, \'\')\n\n  const messages = [\n    {role: \'system\', content: systemPrompt},\n    ...history.slice(-10),\n    {role: \'user\', content: message},\n  ]\n\n  const res = await fetch(`${baseUrl}/chat/completions`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: {\n      \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n      \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,\n    },\n    body: JSON.stringify({\n      model: \'MiniMax-M2.7-highspeed\',\n      messages,\n      temperature: 0.7,\n      max_tokens: 4096,\n    }),\n  })\n\n  if (!res.ok) {\n    const errText = await res.text()\n    throw new Error(`MiniMax HTTP ${res.status}: ${errText}`)\n  }\n\n  const data = await res.json()\n  const rawContent = data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || \'\'\n  const content = stripThinking(rawContent)\n  console.log(\'[MiniMax raw]\', rawContent.slice(0, 300))\n  console.log(\'[MiniMax stripped]\', content.slice(0, 300))\n\n  if (looksAbnormal(content)) {\n    throw new Error(`MiniMax returned abnormal content: ${content.slice(0, 100)}`)\n  }\n\n  return content\n}\n\n// ── 灰色地带：让 LLM 做语义判断（返回结构化 JSON）────────────────\nasync function llmJudge(\n  userInput: string,\n  history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>,\n): Promise<{action: GuardAction; task_type: TaskType; reason: string}> {\n  let raw = \'\'\n  try {\n    raw = await callMiniMax(\n      `请判断以下用户输入的意图：\\n\\n"${userInput}"\\n\\n只返回 JSON，不要其他内容。`,\n      history,\n      GUARD_JUDGE_PROMPT,\n    )\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error(\'[llmJudge] callMiniMax failed:\', e)\n    // 调用失败默认放行对话（保护创作体验优先）\n    return {action: \'allow_chat\', task_type: \'normal_chat\', reason: \'LLM call failed, default allow\'}\n  }\n\n  const parsed = extractJSON(raw)\n  if (parsed && typeof parsed.action === \'string\') {\n    return {\n      action: (parsed.action as GuardAction) || \'allow_chat\',\n      task_type: (parsed.task_type as TaskType) || \'normal_chat\',\n      reason: (parsed.reason as string) || \'\',\n    }\n  }\n  // JSON 解析失败 → 默认放行（白名单优先原则）\n  console.warn(\'[llmJudge] JSON parse failed, raw:\', raw.slice(0, 200))\n  return {action: \'allow_chat\', task_type: \'normal_chat\', reason: \'JSON parse failed, default allow\'}\n}\n\n// ── 附件 metadata 类型（与前端 AttachmentMeta 对应）─────────────\ninterface AttachmentMeta {\n  type: \'image\' | \'file\' | \'video\'\n  file_url: string\n  file_key: string\n  mime_type: string\n  file_type: string\n  name: string\n  size?: number\n}\n\n// ── 调用 luna_hermes_chat（内部 Edge Function）────────────────────\nasync function callHermes(params: {\n  systemPrompt: string\n  userMessage: string\n  history: Array<{role: string; content: string}>\n  attachments: AttachmentMeta[]\n  taskType: TaskType\n  platforms: string[]\n  goal: string\n  materialText: string\n  industry: string\n  authHeader: string\n  supabaseUrl: string\n  serviceRoleKey: string\n}): Promise<string> {\n  const url = `${params.supabaseUrl}/functions/v1/luna_hermes_chat`\n  const res = await fetch(url, {\n    method: => \'\')\n    throw new Error(`luna_hermes_chat HTTP ${res.status}: ${errText}`)\n  }\n  const data = await res.json()\n  return data.reply || \'\'\n}\n\n// ── 主处理逻辑 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nDeno.serve(async (req: Request) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(\'ok\', {headers: CORS})\n\n  // 路由日志：入口\n  console.log(\'[luna_route] entry = luna_guardian\')\n\n  try {\n    const supabaseUrl = Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_URL\')!\n    const serviceRoleKey = Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\')!\n (Array.isArray(body.attachments) && (body.attachments as AttachmentMeta[]).length > 0) {\n      attachments = body.attachments as AttachmentMeta[]\n    } else {\n      // 兼容旧格式：material_images / attachments.push({type: \'file\', file_url: legacyFile, file_key: \'\', mime_type: \'application/octet-stream\', file_type: ext, name: `文件.${ext}`})\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 安保检测仅针对文字输入；文件/图片 URL 不参与安保，只在生成阶段使用\n    const userMessage = (body.user_message as string || body.material_text as string || \'\').trim()\n    const allInputText = [body.material_text, body.industry, body.user_message, hit →\', whitelistAction)\n      guardAction = whitelistAction\n      guardTaskType = inferTaskType(body)\n    } else {\n      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n      // 第二层：黑名单快拦截（不调 LLM，第二快）\n      // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n      const blacklisted = checkBlacklist(allInputText || userMessage)\n      if (blacklisted) {\n      1 /**
     2  * luna_hermes_chat — Hermes 调用适配器
     3  *
     4  * 职责：
     5  *  1. 接收 luna_guardian 路由过来的请求（system_prompt / messages / task_type / attachments / 生成参数）
     6  *  2. 将 attachments 按类型整理进 Hermes prompt
     7  *     - 图片：在 user 消息末尾追加 "用户附上了图片：<url>"（Hermes 不支持 image_url 对象）
     8  *     - 文档：追加 "用户附上了文件「name」，地址：<url>，请基于该文件内容生成"
     9  *     - 视频：第一版提示用户补充说明，文件 URL 保存备查
    10  *  3. 调用 Hermes POST /v1/chat/completions
    11  *  4. 返回统一格式：{ reply, model, upstream, raw }
    12  *
    13  * 安全：HERMES_API_KEY 只在此函数内读取，不暴露给前端或其他 Edge Function。
    14  */
    15 
    16 import {createClient} from 'jsr:@supabase/supabase-js@2'

    18 const CORS = {
    19   'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
    20   'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',

    24 const DEFAULT_HERMES_BASE_URL = 'http://152.136.47.2:8642'
